          <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
           <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://chicago.suntimes.com/politics/2021/3/20/22341909/pritzker-reelection-campaign-contribution">
            Pritzker signals reelection bid with $35M campaign contribution
           </a>
          </h2>
          <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
           The billionaire governor has not publicly confirmed he’s running again in 2022, saying his top priority is managing the state through the COVID-19 pandemic.

          <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
           <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://chicago.suntimes.com/crime/2021/3/21/22343135/tracey-thomas-attempted-murder-charges-swat-team-standoff-person-shot-lacrosse-street-austin">
            Man charged with attempted murder after shooting CPD officer, sparking West Side SWAT standoff: police
           </a>
          </h2>
          <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
           The officers were investigating reports of shots fired about 11:30 a.m. near Lake Street and Cicero Avenue when Tracey Thomas Jr., 29, allegedly opened fire on them, Chicago police said.
          </p>

          <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
           <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://chicago.suntimes.com/sports/2021/3/21/22343275/loyola-upsets-top-seeded-illinois">
            Loyola upsets No. 1-seeded Illinois 71-58 in second round of NCAA Tournament
           </a>
          </h2>
          <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
           Illinois loses to Loyola Chicago 71-58 in second round of NCAA Tournament, becoming first No. 1 seed to be ousted.
          </p>
          <div class="c-byline">
           <span class="c-byline-wrapper">
            By
            <span class="c-byline__item">
             <a data-analytics-link="author-name" href="https://chicago.suntimes.com/users/eddie-pells-associated-press-cst">

              </span>
             </a>
            </span>
           </span>

          <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
           <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://chicago.suntimes.com/2021/3/21/22339826/chicago-police-elected-commission-lori-lightfoot">
            About that magical commission that would solve Chicago’s policing problems
           </a>
          </h2>
          <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
           When it comes to one of the toughest jobs in Chicago, running and reforming the police department, another layer of semi-anonymous government is no way to go.
          </p>
          <div class="c-byline">
           <span class="c-byline-wrapper">

          <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
           <a data-analytics-link="feature" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://chicago.suntimes.com/2021/3/19/22337073/patrick-daley-thompson-uptown-pensacola-place-scotland-yard-washington-federal-bank-savings">
            Ald. Patrick Daley Thompson voted to OK development of a property he’d sold months earlier
           </a>
          </h2>
          <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
           The Bridgeport alderman — also under investigation for possible tax fraud — didn’t disclose his stake in Pensacola Place apartments or a second Uptown property until six months after the council vote.
          </p>

           <span class="c-byline-wrapper">

         <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
          <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://chicago.suntimes.com/columnists/2021/3/19/22340913/kevin-sconiers-west-side-chicago-sconsongs-john-fountain">
           Songs of hope and soul from a fellow West  Sider
          </a>
         </h2>
         <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
          Kevin Sconiers music was nurtured in a Black Chicago-bred creative spirit that captures slices of life that reverberate through time.
         </p>

         <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
          <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://chicago.suntimes.com/columnists/2021/3/19/22340863/loretto-hospital-covid-coronavirus-vaccine-shots-misuse">
           Loretto Hospital leaders deserve more than a ‘harsh reprimand’ for misuse of COVID shots
          </a>
         </h2>
         <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
          Even if they misunderstood the guidelines, there’s no excuse for not knowing their primary mission should be to provide for the predominantly Black community the hospital serves.
         </p>

          <img alt="Mark Brown" class="c-dynamic-image" data-cdata="{}" data-chorus-optimize-field="main_image" data-cid="site/dynamic_size_image-1616355575_7015_344595" src="https://cdn.vox-cdn.com/thumbor/HxDSjXywJasVyM10cfNcq13DPzo=/512x512/cdn.vox-cdn.com/author_profile_images/192541/Mark_Brown.0.jpg"/>
          <noscript>
          </noscript>

        </a>

         <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
          <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://chicago.suntimes.com/columnists/2021/3/19/22340805/parking-meters-montrose-harbor">
           Why I’m serious about keeping parking meters away from Montrose Harbor
          </a>
         </h2>
         <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
          Having to pay $2.25 an hour to park is going to keep some regulars from coming — like the families from all over the city who bring their kids for picnics near the beach.
         </p>
         <div class="c-byline" data-cdata='{"timestamp":1616189400}' data-cid="site/byline-1616355575_3860_344597">

          </a>
         </h2>

           </a>
          </h2>
          <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">

            <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
             <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://chicago.suntimes.com/politics/2021/3/21/22341405/fact-check-american-rescue-plan-covid-19-coronavirus-relief-mike-bost-states-checks-balances">
              Fact-check: Democrats’ relief bill doesn’t give states free hand in spending — but it doesn’t tie them very tight either
             </a>
            </h2>
            <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
             The law — dubbed the "American Rescue Plan" by President Joe Biden — is more flexible than previous aid packages in how money can be spent, experts told us. But it’s also not a free-for-all.
            </p>

            </ul>
            <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
             <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://chicago.suntimes.com/crime/2021/3/21/22342997/man-killed-forest-park-shooting">

             </a>
            </h2>
            <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
             The 25-year-old was found with a gunshot wound in a vehicle parked near the Harlem/Lake Green Line station, police said.

             </a>
            </h2>
            <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
             Karl Cooks surrendered to police about 6:45 a.m., after barricading himself inside a home in Joliet.
            </p>
            <div class="c-byline" data-cdata='{"timestamp":1616285137}' data-cid="site/byline-1616355302_9803_265803">
             <span class="c-byline-wrapper">
              By
              <span class="c-byline__item">
               <a data-analytics-link="author-name" href="https://chicago.suntimes.com/authors/sun-times-wire">
                <span class="c-byline__author-name">
                 Sun-Times Wire
                </span>
               </a>
              </span>
              <span class="c-byline__item">
               <time class="c-byline__item" data-relative-timestamp="true" data-ui="timestamp" datetime="2021-03-21T00:05:37">
                March 20
               </time>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="c-byline__gear">
              <a data-cdata='{"id":22106402}' data-cid="tools/entry_admin_button-1616355302_7438_265802" data-entry-admin="22106402">
              </a>
             </span>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>

            <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
             <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://chicago.suntimes.com/crime/2021/3/19/22341386/loop-stabbing-man-critically-wounded-randolph">
              Man critically wounded in Loop stabbing
             </a>
            </h2>
            <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
             Someone walked up and stabbed the man in the abdomen about 8:35 p.m. as he walked with another person in the first block of East Randolph Street, Chicago police said.
            </p>
